### [1] [VLADriver-RAG: Retrieval-Augmented Vision-Language-Action Models for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08133)
*Rui Zhao,Haofeng Hu,Zhenhai Gao,Jiaqiao Liu,Gao Fei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VLADriver-RAG，将检索增强引入视觉-语言-行动自动驾驶，利用情景图检索和对齐以提升长尾泛化，达到SOTA（Bench2Drive驾驶分89.12）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端VLA在长尾场景泛化差，隐式参数化知识难覆盖；传统视觉检索RAG延迟高且语义歧义，难以为规划提供稳定外部先验。

Method: 1) Visual-to-Scenario：将多模态感知抽象为时空语义图，去除视觉噪声并结构化表征；2) Scenario-Aligned Embedding：基于图的表示学习，并用Graph-DTW进行度量对齐，强调拓扑一致性优先于表面视觉相似；3) 检索先验融合：在查询式VLA骨干中融合检索到的结构化先验，合成精确、解耦的轨迹。

Result: 在Bench2Drive上取得新的SOTA，Driving Score为89.12，并在多种复杂场景中展现更高的相关性检索、更低延迟与更稳定规划（摘要未给出具体消融）。

Conclusion: 结构化情景图+Graph-DTW对齐的RAG能有效为VLA提供可靠外部先验，提升端到端自动驾驶在长尾与复杂场景的泛化与规划质量。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have emerged as a promising paradigm for end-to-end autonomous driving, yet their reliance on implicit parametric knowledge limits generalization in long-tail scenarios. While Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) offers a solution by accessing external expert priors, standard visual retrieval suffers from high latency and semantic ambiguity. To address these challenges, we propose \textbf{VLADriver-RAG}, a framework that grounds planning in explicit, structure-aware historical knowledge. Specifically, we abstract sensory inputs into spatiotemporal semantic graphs via a \textit{Visual-to-Scenario} mechanism, effectively filtering visual noise. To ensure retrieval relevance, we employ a \textit{Scenario-Aligned Embedding Model} that utilizes Graph-DTW metric alignment to prioritize intrinsic topological consistency over superficial visual similarity. These retrieved priors are then fused within a query-based VLA backbone to synthesize precise, disentangled trajectories. Extensive experiments on the Bench2Drive benchmark establish a new state-of-the-art, achieving a Driving Score of 89.12.

</details>


### [2] [Benchmarking ResNet Backbones in RT-DETR: Impact of Depth and Regularization under environmental conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08136)
*Pamela Barboza,Víctor Castelli,Belén Pereira,Ricardo Grando,Bruna de Vargas,Augusto Calfani*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文比较RT-DETR在竞赛机器人环境下识别圆形目标时，对不同ResNet骨干与环境/超参数变化的鲁棒性；发现光照与背景变化主要影响置信度而非时延，准确率几乎满分；在不同环境下，中等深度模型最均衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在竞赛机器人中，视觉系统必须在光照与背景频繁变化下保持实时、稳定的检测。现有基于Transformer的检测器研究较少系统分析骨干规模、Dropout与环境因素对性能（置信度、准确率、时延）的影响，因此需要定量比较以指导模型与部署选择。

Method: 采用RT-DETR作为检测框架，分别接入四种ResNet骨干（18/34/50/101），在相同训练配置下训练，并引入不同Dropout率。测试阶段分别施加两类环境扰动：光照变化与背景对比度变化。评估指标包括分类准确率、预测置信度与推理时延。

Result: 环境变化主要降低预测置信度，对推理时延影响很小，分类准确率几乎始终接近或达到1.00。两种环境下出现不同最优：光照变化时，ResNet50在准确率近乎完美、置信度最高约0.869、时延约0.058-0.059 ms之间取得最佳权衡；背景变化时，ResNet34更均衡，准确率近乎完美、置信度最高约0.887。

Conclusion: 最优架构取决于具体环境扰动类型；在该任务上，中等深度骨干（ResNet34/50）在性能与效率间更具优势。应根据预期的光照或背景变化选择骨干，Dropout与环境对置信度影响更显著，而准确率与时延相对稳定。

Abstract: Visual perception plays a central role in competitive robotics, where environmental variations can directly affect real-time detection performance. The related literature on transformer-based detectors lack information regarding the impact of backbone scale and environmental settings on model performance. This work presents a comparative evaluation of RT-DETR for detecting round objects under environmental and hyperparameter variations relevant to competitive robotics. Four ResNet backbones (ResNet18, ResNet34, ResNet50, and ResNet101) were compared using dropout rates, analyzing their effect on confidence and accuracy. All models were trained under the same configuration and evaluated under changes in lighting and background contrast. Environmental conditions primarily impact prediction confidence, while inference latency remains largely unaffected and classification accuracy stays consistently high, approaching or above 1.00 in most cases. Two distinct behaviors were observed. Under illumination variation, ResNet50 achieves the best trade-off, combining near-perfect accuracy, confidence values up to approximately 0.869 and latency around 0.058-0.059 ms. Under background variation, ResNet34 provides the most balanced performance, reaching near-perfect accuracy and higher confidence values up to approximately 0.887. These results indicate that the optimal architecture depends on the type of environmental variation, with intermediate-depth models offering the best balance between performance and efficiency.

</details>


### [3] [Self-Captioning Multimodal Interaction Tuning: Amplifying Exploitable Redundancies for Robust Vision Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08145)
*Yuriel Ryan,Hei Man Ip,Adriel Kuek,Paul Pu Liang,Roy Ka-Wei Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出通过增强模态间“冗余”共享信息来缓解VLM的幻觉与脆弱性；用自标注流程与“多模态交互门”将独有信息转化为冗余信息，显著降低视觉诱发错误并提升一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型在面对歧义或受损模态时易产生幻觉和不稳健。作者认为可利用模态间共享信息来补偿受损模态，但当前指令数据集为强调视觉对齐常去除冗余，削弱了这种补偿能力。

Method: 提出分析并操控三类多模态交互：冗余（共享）、独有（各自专属）、协同（涌现）。设计自描述/自标注工作流，并引入“多模态交互门”（Multimodal Interaction Gate, MIG），将独有信息转化为冗余信息，从而在训练数据或模型处理中放大冗余交互。

Result: 通过增加冗余，视觉诱发错误下降38.3%，一致性提升16.8%。

Conclusion: 增强模态冗余是提升VLM可靠性与一致性的有效途径；通过MIG与自标注可在不牺牲任务相关性下缓解幻觉与对受损模态的脆弱性。

Abstract: Current vision language models face hallucination and robustness issues against ambiguous or corrupted modalities. We hypothesize that these issues can be addressed by exploiting the shared information between modalities to compensate for the impaired one. To this end, we analyze multimodal interactions -- redundant (shared), unique (exclusive), and synergistic (emergent) task-relevant information provided by the modalities -- to determine their impacts on model reliability. Specifically, amplifying redundant interactions would increase this exploitable shared information to resolve these issues; yet, modern instruction datasets often eliminate redundancies to prioritize visual grounding. We bridge this gap through a self-captioning workflow featuring a \textsc{Multimodal Interaction Gate}: a mechanism to convert unique interactions into redundant interactions. Our findings suggest that increasing redundancy can reduce visual induced errors by 38.3\% and improve consistency by 16.8\%.

</details>


### [4] [VT-Bench: A Unified Benchmark for Visual-Tabular Multi-Modal Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08146)
*Zi-Yi Jia,Zi-Jian Cheng,Xin-Yue Zhang,Kun-Yang Yu,Zhi Zhou,Yu-Feng Li,Lan-Zhe Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VT-Bench，首个统一的视觉-表格任务基准，覆盖14数据集/9领域/75.6万样本，评测23种模型，揭示视觉-表格学习的显著挑战，旨在推动更强大的多模态基础模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉-文本多模态研究成熟，但在医疗与工业等高风险场景常见的“视觉+表格”数据组合研究稀缺，缺乏统一标准来比较判别与生成推理能力，阻碍方法发展与客观评测。

Method: 构建VT-Bench：整合14个跨9领域（以医疗为主，含宠物、媒体、交通）的视觉-表格数据集，总计约75.6万样本；定义统一的判别预测与生成式推理任务协议；选取并系统评测23个代表性模型，覆盖单模态专家、专用视觉-表格模型、通用VLM及工具增强方法。

Result: 系统评测显示，现有模型在视觉-表格任务上存在明显性能瓶颈与泛化不足；不同范式（专家模型、VLM、工具增强）在任务与领域间表现差异大，尚无一类方法在各任务上占优。

Conclusion: VT-Bench为视觉-表格学习提供首个统一评测平台，揭示关键挑战并为后续算法设计与多模态基础模型训练提供方向，期望推动更强大的视觉-表格多模态模型的研究。

Abstract: Multi-model learning has attracted great attention in visual-text tasks. However, visual-tabular data, which plays a pivotal role in high-stakes domains like healthcare and industry, remains underexplored. In this paper, we introduce \textit{VT-Bench}, the first unified benchmark for standardizing vision-tabular discriminative prediction and generative reasoning tasks. VT-Bench aggregates 14 datasets across 9 domains (medical-centric, while covering pets, media, and transportation) with over 756K samples. We evaluate 23 representative models, including unimodal experts, specialized visual-tabular models, general-purpose vision-language models (VLMs), and tool-augmented methods, highlighting substantial challenges of visual-tabular learning. We believe VT-Bench will stimulate the community to build more powerful multi-modal vision-tabular foundation models.
  Benchmark: https://github.com/Ziyi-Jia990/VT-Bench

</details>


### [5] [LAGO: Language-Guided Adaptive Object-Region Focus for Zero-Shot Visual-Text Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08156)
*Junyi Hu,Qiji Zhou,Lei Zhang,Yue Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LAGO提出一种高效稳健的零样本细粒度识别：先无语义的目标候选发现，后按置信度自适应引入语言指导，并用目标-上下文双通道聚合，多证据融合，以更少候选实现SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细粒度零样本识别的判别证据多在局部区域而非整图；现有方法用大量随机/冗余裁剪比对，成本高且噪声大；过早的语义引导易形成“预测环”，将早期错误放大并固化。需要一种既稳健又高效的局部对齐框架。

Method: 提出LAGO框架：1) 类无关、目标中心的候选区域发现，提供稳定视觉初始化；2) 语言引导的自适应细化，根据中间置信度调节语义引导强度，避免错误放大；3) 目标级、上下文及整图证据的双通道聚合，融合多粒度信息；4) 用显著更少候选区域完成视觉-文本对齐与分类。

Result: 在标准零样本基准与分布移位场景上取得一致的SOTA性能，同时显著减少推理时所需候选区域数量，提升效率与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 通过先稳后精、置信度调控与目标-上下文双通道融合，LAGO在低候选、高效率条件下实现稳健的细粒度零样本对齐与识别，缓解预测环问题并推广性更强。

Abstract: Zero-shot recognition aims to classify an image by selecting the most compatible label description from a set of candidate classes without any task-specific supervision. In fine-grained settings, however, the relevant evidence often lies in localized parts, attributes, or textures rather than in the full image, making whole-image alignment suboptimal. Recent localized visual-text alignment methods address this by comparing class descriptions with multiple image regions, but they typically rely on large sets of random or redundant crops, increasing inference cost and introducing many highly redundant or weakly relevant candidates. Moreover, introducing semantic guidance too early can create an error-amplifying feedback process in which inaccurate intermediate predictions bias later localization and reinforce subsequent mistakes; we refer to this failure mode as the prediction loop. We propose LAGO (LAnguage-Guided adaptive Object-region focus), a framework for efficient and robust zero-shot localized visual-text alignment. LAGO first performs class-agnostic object-centric candidate discovery to obtain a stable visual initialization, and then applies adaptive language-guided refinement with the strength of semantic guidance controlled by intermediate confidence. It further combines object-level, contextual, and full-image evidence through an effective object-context dual-channel aggregation strategy. Extensive experiments show that LAGO consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance on standard zero-shot benchmarks and challenging distribution-shift settings, while requiring substantially fewer candidate regions at inference time.

</details>


### [6] [HY-Himmel Technical Report: Hierarchical Interleaved Multi-stream Motion Encoding for Long Video Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08158)
*Haopeng Jin,Hongzhu Yi,Wenlong Zhao,Jinwen Luo,Shani Ye,Zhenyu Guan,Shiquan Dong,Tiankun Yang,Tao Yu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HY-Himmel：分层视频-语言框架，用稀疏I帧给重型ViT做语义锚点，密集间隔用压缩域三流适配器提取运动并与视觉骨干对齐，将运动token注入LLM。以更少token超越32帧致密基线，验证三流必要充分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长视频理解在多模态LLM中受三重瓶颈：解码密集RGB帧代价大；随帧数二次方增长的token预算；稀疏关键帧采样导致运动感知弱。需要一种既节省计算/上下文，又提升运动建模的方案。

Method: 分层分配语义与运动容量：少量稀疏锚点I帧送入高成本ViT以建模对象与场景；在两锚点间的密集帧，工作在压缩域，利用三流适配器（运动向量图、残差图、I帧上下文）蒸馏运动证据为对齐的运动token。通过可微占位符机制将运动token注入LLM；在Stage-1进行对比式对齐训练，使运动表征与冻结视觉骨干几何兼容；应用LoRA等轻量化调优。

Result: 在Video-MME上，相比致密32帧基线，准确率从61.2%提升到63.5%（+2.3个百分点），同时上下文token减少3.6倍。消融研究覆盖流组合、运动编码器族、融合方式、对齐目标、锚点数量、LoRA秩、视频时长，显示三流全量配置带来全部增益。

Conclusion: HY-Himmel通过语义-运动解耦与压缩域三流运动建模，在更低token/计算下提升长视频理解性能；三流设计是达成增益的关键，方法可作为长视频多模态LLM的高效范式。

Abstract: Long-video understanding with multimodal language models suffers from three compounding bottlenecks: heavy decode cost to obtain dense RGB frames, quadratic token growth with frame count, and weak motion perception under sparse keyframe sampling. We present HY-Himmel, a hierarchical video-language framework that allocates semantic and motion capacity separately. A small set of sparse anchor I-frames is routed to the expensive host ViT to ground object identity and scene layout, while the far denser inter-frame intervals are encoded by a lightweight compressed-domain tri-stream adapter that distils motion evidence from motion-vector maps, residual maps, and I-frame context into aligned motion tokens. These tokens are injected into the LLM via a differentiable placeholder mechanism after a dedicated Stage-1 contrastive alignment that places the motion representation in a geometry compatible with the frozen visual backbone. On Video-MME, HY-Himmel surpasses the dense 32-frame baseline by +2.3 pp (61.2 to 63.5%) while using 3.6x fewer context tokens. Extensive ablations over stream composition, motion encoder family, fusion mode, alignment objective, anchor count, LoRA rank, and video duration confirm that the full tri-stream is necessary and sufficient for the observed gains.

</details>


### [7] [WATCH: Wide-Area Archaeological Site Tracking for Change Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08160)
*Girmaw Abebe Tadesse,Titien Bartette,Andrew Hassanali,Allen Kim,Jonathan Chemla,Andrew Zolli,Yves Ubelmann,Caleb Robinson,Inbal Becker-Reshef,Juan Lavista Ferres*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出WATCH框架，用月尺度在PlanetScope拼接影像上定位考古遗址干扰事件，包含三类评分：无训练的TED、自监督SSCD、弱监督WS；在阿富汗1943处遗址及跨区域评测中，无监督优于弱监督；TED+SatMAE月精确召回55%，多个模型在三个月容差内达92.5%；方向性分析揭示SSCD偏早预警、TED偏事后确认；证实基础模型嵌入+卫星影像可规模化监测文化遗产。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 保护文化遗产需要规模化监测考古遗址，但扰动发生时间难以精确定位：视觉线索微弱、标注稀缺。需要一种能在弱标注甚至无标注条件下，于时间序列遥感数据中定位变化月份的方法，并评估不同视觉基础模型的可迁移性和实用性。

Method: 构建WATCH框架，基于PlanetScope月度马赛克（2017–2024, 4.7 m/px）。提供三种互补打分途径：1) TED：以本地时间参考计算月-月嵌入距离，无需训练；2) SSCD：自监督集成，融合重建、预测与潜变量新颖度信号；3) 弱监督WS：用稀疏事件月份标签训练时间定位模型。对1943处阿富汗遗址，比较六类基础模型嵌入（CLIP、GeoRSCLIP、SatMAE、Prithvi-EO-2.0、DINOv3、Satlas-Pretrain）与手工光谱/纹理基线，并做跨区域泛化（叙利亚、土耳其、巴基斯坦、埃及）。提出方向性边际分析评估早预警与事后确认倾向。

Result: 无监督（TED、SSCD）整体优于弱监督。TED+SatMAE在精确月召回达55%（m=0）；TED与GeoRSCLIP/CLIP/Satlas-Pretrain在±3个月容差内召回达92.5%（m=3）。在弱监督设定下，手工特征在精确月检测仍具竞争力。方向性分析：SSCD+GeoRSCLIP或Prithvi-EO-2.0更偏早预警；TED更偏变更发生后的确认。

Conclusion: 基础模型嵌入结合月度卫星影像，可在缺乏标注的情境下实现可扩展且决策相关的遗产监测。WATCH提供多策略月级定位，兼顾早预警与事后确认，具跨区域泛化潜力；代码已开源以促进应用。

Abstract: Monitoring archaeological sites at scale is vital for protecting cultural heritage, yet pinpointing when disturbances occur remains difficult because visual cues are subtle and ground-truth data are sparse. We introduce WATCH, a framework for month-level change-event localization over PlanetScope satellite mosaics (2017-2024, 4.7 m/px) that supports three complementary scoring approaches: (i) Temporal Embedding Distance (TED), a training-free method that scores month-to-month deviations from a local temporal reference; (ii) Self-Supervised Change Detection (SSCD), an ensemble of reconstruction, forecasting, and latent-novelty signals; and (iii) a Weakly Supervised (WS) temporal localization model trained with sparse event-month labels. We benchmark WATCH on 1,943 archaeological sites in Afghanistan using embeddings from six foundation models (CLIP, GeoRSCLIP, SatMAE, Prithvi-EO-2.0, DINOv3, and Satlas-Pretrain) alongside a handcrafted spectral and texture baseline, and assess cross-regional generalization on sites in Syria, Turkey, Pakistan, and Egypt. The unsupervised approaches (TED, SSCD) consistently outperform the weakly supervised alternative. TED with SatMAE achieves the highest exact-month recall (55% at m=0), while TED with GeoRSCLIP, CLIP, or Satlas-Pretrain reaches 92.5% within a three-month tolerance (m=3). Handcrafted features remain competitive for exact-month detection under weak supervision. Our directional margin analysis reveals systematic temporal biases: SSCD paired with GeoRSCLIP or Prithvi-EO-2.0 exhibits the strongest early-warning profile, detecting anomalies before the recorded event, while TED favors confirmation-oriented detection after a change has materialized. These results show that satellite imagery combined with foundation-model embeddings enables scalable, decision-relevant heritage monitoring. Code: https://github.com/microsoft/WATCH

</details>


### [8] [Advanced Tumor Segmentation in PET/CT Imaging: A Training Strategy Study with nnU-Net for AutoPET III](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08161)
*Hussain Alasmawi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出基于nnU-Net（ResNet编码器）的全身PET/CT肿瘤自动分割方案，系统评估归一化、Batch Dice优化与CraveMix增强；显著降低误检、增强对病灶差异的鲁棒性，预测试Dice最高0.80，AutoPET III排名第3。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全身PET/CT肿瘤分割对评估与治疗规划关键，但病灶大小、对比度与解剖分布差异大，手工分割耗时且一致性差；挑战赛目标是跨示踪剂与多中心泛化，亟需稳健自动方法。

Method: 以nnU-Net为基线，采用ResNet编码器；系统对训练策略做消融：强度归一化、Batch Dice损失优化、CraveMix数据增强；在AutoPET III数据框架下评估对误检与变异性的影响。

Result: 最优配置在预测试阶段Dice达0.80，显著减少假阳性并提升对病灶变异的鲁棒性；方法在AutoPET III挑战中排名第三。

Conclusion: 合适的训练策略（归一化、损失设计、混合增强）对提升全身PET/CT肿瘤分割的泛化性与可靠性至关重要；所提方案在多中心、多示踪剂场景下表现稳健并达到领先水平，代码已开源。

Abstract: Tumor segmentation in whole-body PET/CT imaging is crucial for precise disease evaluation and treatment planning. However, it remains challenging due to variability in lesion size, contrast, and anatomical distribution. Relying on manual segmentation makes the process time-consuming and prone to intra- and inter-observer variability. This work presents a whole-body tumor segmentation method developed for the AutoPET III challenge, where the goal is to build models that generalize across tracers and multi-center data. We employ the nnU-Net framework with a ResNet-based encoder as our baseline and systematically investigate the impact of training strategies, including intensity normalization, batch dice optimization, and data augmentation using CraveMix. Our experiments show that these strategies significantly influence model performance, particularly in reducing false positives and improving robustness to lesion variability. The best-performing configuration achieves a Dice score of up to 0.80 on the preliminary test phase, and our method ranked third in the AutoPET III challenge. The code is publicly available here.

### [9] [MULTITEXTEDIT: Benchmarking Cross-Lingual Degradation in Text-in-Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08163)
*Liwei Cheng,Zirui Song,Shibo Feng,Lunjie Zhou,Yixuan Guan,Dayan Guan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MULTITEXTEDIT基准与LSF语言忠实度指标，系统性评测多语言文本内图像编辑，揭示所有模型在跨语言尤其希伯来语/阿拉伯语上的显著退化，问题集中于文本准确与书写体系忠实而非整体布局。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本内图像编辑评测以英语为主，且常把视觉合理性与语义正确性混淆，难以发现细粒度脚本层面错误（如变音符缺失、RTL顺序反转、混用脚本）。需要一个受控、跨语言的基准与能捕获脚本细节的度量。

Method: 构建包含3,600个实例的受控基准，覆盖12种语言、5个视觉域、7种编辑操作；同一视觉底图配多语言变体，并提供人工编辑参考与区域掩码以隔离语言变量。提出两阶段LVM评分类器作为LSF指标：先描摹编辑目标文本再独立判别其正确性；并与母语者标注比对达加权Kappa 0.76。

Conclusion: 多语言文本内图像编辑的关键瓶颈在脚本与文本层面的忠实度。MULTITEXTEDIT与LSF补足现有评测缺口，可更可靠地比较跨语言性能，并提示未来模型需专注于RTL处理、变音与脚本渲染等细节。

Abstract: Text-in-image editing has become a key capability for visual content creation, yet existing benchmarks remain overwhelmingly English-centric and often conflate visual plausibility with semantic correctness. We introduce MULTITEXTEDIT, a controlled benchmark of 3,600 instances spanning 12 typologically diverse languages, 5 visual domains, and 7 editing operations. Language variants of each instance share a common visual base and are paired with a human-edited reference and region masks, isolating the language variable for cross-lingual comparison. To capture script-level errors that coarse text-matching metrics miss, such as missing diacritics, reversed RTL order, and mixed-script renderings, we introduce a language fidelity (LSF) metric scored by a two-stage LVM protocol that first traces the edited target text and then judges it in isolation, reaching a quadratic-weighted \k{appa} of 0.76 against native-speaker annotators. Evaluating 12 open-source and proprietary systems with LSF alongside standard semantic and mask-aware pixel metrics, we find pronounced cross-lingual degradation for every model, largest on Hebrew and Arabic and smallest on Dutch and Spanish, and concentrated in text accuracy and script fidelity rather than in coarse structural dimensions. We also uncover a pervasive semantic and pixel mismatch, where outputs preserve global layout and background fidelity yet distort script-specific forms.

In addition, a model-specific adaptive threshold optimization strategy based on the Youden Index is employed to improve classification reliability by achieving a better balance between true positive and false positive rates.
  Experiments conducted on the CASIA v2.0 dataset using multiple pretrained CNN architectures, including DenseNet121, VGG16, ResNet50, EfficientNetB0, MobileNet, and InceptionV3, demonstrate the effectiveness and robustness of the proposed framework. The models are evaluated using comprehensive performance metrics such as accuracy, precision, recall, F1-score, Matthews correlation coefficient (MCC), and area under the ROC curve (AUC).
  The results show that DenseNet121 achieves the highest accuracy and AUC, while ResNet50 provides the most balanced and reliable predictions with the highest MCC. Overall, the proposed framework improves the visibility of manipulation artifacts and enhances classification robustness, making it suitable for real-world digital image forgery detection scenarios.

### [12] [Augmented Equivariant Mesh Networks for Anatomical Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08172)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗网格分割需直接处理不规则曲面，且对患者姿态和网格分辨率变化鲁棒。现有点云/网格方法通常不具等变性，测试时对旋转/倾斜等扰动性能大幅下降（如40°倾斜IoU下降25-26点）。

Method: 构建EAMS（Equivariant Anatomical Mesh Segmentor），以等变网格神经网络为基础；融合内在网格描述符与解剖先验（如牙弓与肝表面基于PCA的参考框架）；在消息传递中加入轻量级全局上下文；在四个任务上评估，覆盖边、点、面级监督。

Result: 在颅内动脉瘤与口内扫描分割任务上，EAMS在未扰动输入上与专用基线性能相当，同时在几何扰动下保持稳定；在肝表面任务上展现了标准姿态精度与旋转鲁棒性之间更优的折中。整体参数<2M。

Conclusion: 轻量级的等变框架无需任务特定架构即可在多种监督类型与多种临床任务中实现鲁棒的解剖网格分割，尤其对姿态/旋转扰动具有优势。

Abstract: Anatomical mesh segmentation requires models that operate directly on irregular surface geometry while remaining robust to arbitrary patient pose and mesh resolution variation. Existing task-specific mesh and point-cloud methods are not equivariant, and can degrade sharply under test-time perturbation, for example dropping by 25-26 IoU points on intraoral scan segmentation at $40^\circ$ tilt. We present EAMS, an Equivariant Anatomical Mesh Segmentor built on Equivariant Mesh Neural Networks (EMNN), and evaluate it across four clinically distinct tasks spanning edge-, vertex-, and face-level supervision. We combine intrinsic mesh descriptors with anatomy-aware priors, including PCA-derived frames for dental arches and liver surfaces, and augment message passing to provide lightweight global context. Across intracranial aneurysm and intraoral segmentation, EAMS variants are competitive with specialized baselines on unperturbed inputs while remaining stable under geometric perturbations, and on liver surfaces they expose a favorable trade-off between canonical-pose accuracy and rotation robustness. These results show that a lightweight ($<2$M parameters) equivariant framework can deliver robust anatomical mesh segmentation across diverse supervision types without task-specific architectures.

### [13] [CASISR: Circular Arbitrary-Scale Image Super-Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08173)
*Honggui Li,Zhengyang Zhang,Dingtai Li,Sinan Chen,Nahid Md Lokman Hossain,Xinfeng Xu,Yinlu Qin,Ruobing Wang,Hantao Lu,Yuting Feng,Maria Trocan,Dimitri Galayko,Amara Amara,Mohamad Sawan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种闭环“循环ASISR（CASISR）”架构，将ASISR与退化模型组合成闭环，用控制理论提升任意尺度超分辨的泛化；理论上用条件概率与泰勒近似证明合理性与稳定性；实验优于8种SOTA，尤其在分数放大倍率与文本/条纹等剧烈边缘场景显著受益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ASISR在开放环从LR到SR推断，训练数据有限而测试分布无限，导致泛化不足；已知或可学习的退化模型（下采样+噪声）提供了从SR回到LR的通道，因此有机会构造闭环，利用测试样本与一致性约束自适应提升重建质量与泛化。

Method: 构建闭环：SR网络(ASISR)与退化模型串联，形成从LR→SR→LR̂的循环；建立非线性环路方程，引入一致性/反馈误差以校正SR输出；用条件概率论证在给定退化先验下闭环合理性，用泰勒级数分析小扰动下的稳定性；提出一阶/二阶绝对差分图像指标以更敏感地评估边缘与纹理恢复，对比分数尺度重建。

Result: 大量模拟实验表明CASISR在重建质量上全面超过8个SOTA任意尺度SR方法；在分数缩放因子以及含剧烈边缘的文本与条纹图像上优势尤为明显。

Conclusion: 将ASISR与退化模型闭环化能显著提升泛化与重建细节；理论与实验均支持CASISR的有效性与稳定性，特别适合分数倍率与强边缘场景。

Abstract: The generalization performance (GP) of deep learning-based arbitrary-scale image super-resolution (ASISR) methods is subject to limited training datasets and unlimited testing datasets. It is vitally significant to enhance the GP of the pretrained ASISR models by making full use of the testing samples. The ASISR models usually employ an open-loop architecture from low-resolution (LR) images to super-resolution (SR) images. The degradation model from SR samples to LR samples is known bicubic down-sampling for the classical ASISR, is supposed down-sampling with additive random noise for the blind ASISR, and is learnable for the real-world ASISR. Combining the ASISR and degradation models, it is potentially possible to adopt a closed-loop architecture based on the automatic control theory for strengthening the GP of the ASISR methods. Therefore, this paper proposes a closed-loop architecture, circular ASISR (CASISR), to lift the capability of image reconstruction. A mathematical nonlinear loop equation is established to describe the CASISR, the reasonability of the CASISR is proven by conditional probability theory, and the stability of the CASISR is proven by Taylor series approximation. The first-order and second-order absolute difference images are defined to compare the image reconstruction performance of the ASISR and the CASISR methods. Comprehensive simulation experiments show that the proposed CASISR approach outperforms the eight state-of-the-art ASISR approaches in the quality of image reconstruction. Especially, the proposed CASISR is extraordinarily suitable for fractional SR scale factors and is extremely effective for text and stripe images with drastically changed edges.

</details>


### [14] [KARMA-MV: A Benchmark for Causal Question Answering on Music Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08175)
*Archishman Ghosh,Abhinaba Roy,Dorien Herremans*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: KARMA-MV 引入面向音乐视频的因果多模态问答基准，利用LLM生成与校验的多选题，以及因果知识图增强VLM/LLM，在跨模态时序与因果推理上显著提升，尤其利于小模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频问答多聚焦相关性与跨模态理解，缺乏对“视觉动态如何驱动音乐结构”的因果推理能力与可扩展评测。需要一个能覆盖因果、预测、反事实等问题类型的数据集与方法框架。

Method: 1) 构建 KARMA-MV：从 2,682 个 YouTube 音乐视频自动生成与验证 37,737 道多选题，问题覆盖因果推理、预测、反事实；依赖LLM进行可扩展生成和质量控制。2) 提出因果知识图（CKG）：抽取并组织音频-视觉时序事件与其跨模态依赖关系，作为结构化检索信号，增强现有VLM/LLM的推理。3) 在多种最先进模型上接入CKG以评估增益。

Result: 在多种SOTA VLM与LLM上，接入CKG均带来稳定性能提升，且对小模型增益更大，表明显式因果结构能有效支持音乐视频的跨模态因果推理。

Conclusion: KARMA-MV 为音乐视频的因果音视理解提供了首个大规模基准；通过CKG为模型注入显式因果结构，可超越纯相关性学习，提升因果、预测与反事实问答能力。

Abstract: While significant progress has been made in Video Question Answering and cross-modal understanding, causal reasoning about how visual dynamics drive musical structure in music videos remains under-explored. We introduce KARMA-MV, a large-scale multiple-choice QA dataset derived from 2,682 YouTube music videos, designed to test models' ability to integrate temporal audio-visual cues and reason about visual-to-musical influence across reasoning, prediction, and counterfactual questions. Unlike traditional datasets requiring manual annotation, KARMA-MV leverages LLM reasoning for scalable generation and validation, yielding 37,737 MCQs. We propose a causal knowledge graph (CKG) approach that augments vision-language models (VLMs) with structured retrieval of cross-modal dependencies. Experiments on state-of-the-art VLMs and LLMs show consistent gains from CKG grounding -- especially for smaller models -- establishing the value of explicit causal structure for music-video reasoning. KARMA-MV provides a new benchmark for advancing causal audio-visual understanding beyond correlation.

### [15] [Text-Guided Multi-Scale Frequency Representation Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08181)
*Weicai Yan,Xinhua Ma,Wang Lin,Tao Jin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FreqAdapter：在频域进行多尺度参数高效微调，融合文本信息，显著提升CLIP与LLaVA等多模态模型的性能与效率，一轮内快速收敛、开销极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有参数高效微调大多在信号（时域/像素）空间进行，冗余信息大；且常用固定提示或单一适配层，难以覆盖信号的多尺度特性与不同频段的感受野需求，导致适应新分布的表达能力受限。

Method: 提出Multi-Scale Frequency Adapter（FreqAdapter）：1）将信号转换到频域，在不同频率尺度上进行微调，减少冗余；2）跨尺度地融合文本/语义信息；3）设计多尺度适配策略，为不同频段分配合适的感受野与参数；4）以轻量可插拔的适配器形式集成到多模态模型（如CLIP、LLaVA）中。

Result: 在CLIP与LLaVA等多模态任务上进行大量实验，FreqAdapter在保持极小参数与计算开销的同时，显著优于现有方法，并能在1个epoch内快速收敛。

Conclusion: 频域的多尺度参数高效适配能够有效减少冗余并提升跨频段表达能力，进而在多模态场景中带来更高效、更高性能的迁移与微调；方法通用、易集成且训练成本低。

Abstract: Parameter-efficient fine-tuning methods introduce a small number of training parameters, enabling pre-trained models to adapt rapidly to new data distributions. While these methods have shown promising results, they exhibit notable limitations. First, most existing methods operate in the signal space domain, which results in substantial information redundancy. Second, most existing methods utilize fixed prompts or adaptation layers, failing to fully account for the multi-scale characteristics of signals. To address these challenges, we propose the Multi-Scale Frequency Adapter (FreqAdapter), which integrates textual information and performs multi-scale fine-tuning of signals in the frequency domain. Additionally, we introduce a multi-scale adaptation strategy to optimize receptive fields across different frequency ranges, further enhancing the model's representational capacity. Extensive experiments on multimodal models, including CLIP and LLaVA, demonstrate that FreqAdapter significantly improves both performance and efficiency. FreqAdapter improves performance with minimal cost and fast convergence within one epoch. Code is available at https://github.com/Kelvin-ywc/FreqAdapter.

### [16] [Sparsity Hurts: Simple Linear Adapter Can Boost Generalized Category Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08183)
*Bo Ye,Kai Gan,Tong Wei,Min-Ling Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出LAGCD：在每个ViT块中加入线性残差adapter，并配合分布对齐损失，在GCD任务上优于多种强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GCD依赖预训练表示并通过局部微调或视觉prompt来适配下游，但：1）仅微调最后一层可适应性不足；2）视觉prompt易过拟合、依赖初始化且容量受限。需要一种既能全模型适配又避免过拟合的新机制。

Method: 在每个ViT块内嵌一个残差线性adapter（无非线性），提升容量与灵活性；并从特征稀疏性角度论证非线性adapter反而有害。另加入辅助的分布对齐损失以缓解已知/新类预测偏置问题。整体在预训练ViT上进行适配学习。

Result: 在通用与细粒度数据集上进行大量实验，LAGCD在已知类保持分类能力的同时，对未知类发现更优，持续超越多种复杂基线。代码开源。

Conclusion: 线性残差adapter较非线性adapter在GCD更有效；配合分布对齐可减少已知/新类偏置。方法简单、稳定、泛化好，并在多数据集上取得一致提升。

Abstract: Generalized Category Discovery (GCD) seeks to identify novel categories from unlabeled data while retaining the classification ability of seen categories. Prior GCD methods commonly leverage transferable representations from pre-trained models, adapting to downstream datasets via partial fine-tuning (updating only the final ViT block) and visual prompt tuning (appending learnable vectors to inputs). However, conventional partial fine-tuning offers limited flexibility, as it fails to adapt the entire model; meanwhile, visual prompt tuning is prone to overfitting, due to its sensitivity to initialization and inherently constrained capacity. To address these limitations, we propose LAGCD, a simple yet effective GCD approach that embeds a residual linear adapter into each ViT block. From the perspective of feature sparsity, we systematically show that non-linearity in conventional adapters impairs performance, whereas our linear adapter enhances it by enabling more flexible model capacity. We further introduce an auxiliary distribution alignment loss to mitigate the negative impact of biased predictions between seen and novel categories. Extensive experiments on both generic and fine-grained datasets confirm that LAGCD consistently improves performance over many sophisticated baselines. The source code is available at https://github.com/yebo0216best/LAGCD

</details>


### [17] [Neuroscience-Inspired Analyses of Visual Interestingness in Multimodal Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08188)

Main category: cs.CV

Method: 以 Flickr 大规模人类互动数据定义的 Common Interestingness（CI）分数为“视觉有趣度”标签；在 Qwen3-VL-8B 中，对视觉与语言部件的内部表示进行神经科学风格分析：线性可解码性测试、降维与 GDV 判别度分析、概念向量提取（几何/探针/稀疏自编码器三法）及表征相似性分析（RSA），观察 CI 概念在层间的涌现与收敛。

Result: CI 信息能从最终层嵌入线性解码；相关隐藏表示在视觉 Transformer 中层出现，在语言模型层逐步可分离度提升；不同方法得到的“有趣度”概念向量在高层收敛并表现出较高表征相似性，指向稳定、结构化的编码。

Conclusion: Qwen3-VL-8B 在无显式监督下学习到与人类有趣度一致的内在表示。该结果为连接人脑动力学与 Transformer 架构的共享计算原则提供线索，未来可进一步揭示生物与人工系统中注意与兴趣的组织机制。

Abstract: Human attention is the gateway to conscious perception, memory and decision-making. However, its role in modern transformer models remains largely unexplored. As these systems increasingly influence what people see, prefer and buy, the question arises as to whether they encode principles of human interest or merely exploit large-scale correlations. Addressing this issue is crucial for understanding cognition and ensuring the responsible use of AI in communication and marketing. In order to address this issue, the concept of visual interest was examined within the multimodal vision-language-model Qwen3-VL-8B, using a pre-defined Common Interestingness (CI) score derived from large-scale human engagement data on the photo-sharing platform Flickr. Here, we analyzed internal representations across vision and language components using methods from the neurosciences. Our analyses revealed that CI information is linearly decodable from final-layer embeddings, indicating that it is aligned with human-derived measures of visual interestingness. Dimensionality reduction and Generalized Discrimination Value (GDV) analyses demonstrate that CI-related hidden representations emerge in intermediate vision transformer layers and becomes progressively more distinguishable across language model layers. Concept vectors derived using geometric, probe, and Sparse Auto-Encoder based methods converge in higher layers, as confirmed by representational similarity analysis. This indicates a robust and structured encoding of visual interestingness without explicit supervision. Future work will seek to identify shared computational principles linking human brain dynamics and transformer architectures, with the ultimate goal of uncovering the organizing mechanisms that give rise to attention and interest in both biological and artificial systems.

### [18] [A Robust Out-of-Distribution Detection Framework via Synergistic Smoothing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08191)
*Maria Stoica,Abdelrahman Hekal,Alessio Lomuscio*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ROSS，一种鲁棒的后处理式OOD检测器，通过中值平滑与“局部不稳定性”评估，实现对最小化与最大化型对抗攻击的对称鲁棒，较现有方法最高提升约40 AUROC点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OOD检测虽在干净样本上有效，但对对抗攻击极其脆弱，难以满足安全部署需求；需要一种在不改动已训练模型的前提下，能同时抵御不同方向攻击并维持干净性能的鲁棒检测方法。

Method: 1) 先对基线OOD分数施加中值平滑：对输入添加多次小噪声，取分数中位数，以权衡干净与对抗准确率；2) 复用为平滑而生成的噪声样本，度量基线分数在局部扰动下的“不稳定性”（如分数方差/分位差等）；3) 将不稳定性作为新的判别信号，与平滑分数组合形成ROSS分数，从而更好区分ID与OOD；4) 设计为对称防御，同时抑制攻击者试图降低或提高分数的两类目标。

Result: 在CIFAR-10/100与ImageNet上进行广泛实验，相比SOTA在对抗场景下显著提升鲁棒性，最高可提升约40 AUROC点；对干净样本仍保持较强性能；在最小化与最大化型攻击下均取得强劲、对称的鲁棒表现。

Conclusion: 利用局部不稳定性作为额外信号并配合中值平滑，可实现对称且强健的OOD检测，在多数据集上达到新的鲁棒SOTA，且为后处理方法，易于集成与复现（代码公开）。

Abstract: Reliable out-of-distribution (OOD) detection is a critical requirement for the safe deployment of machine learning systems. Despite recent progress, state-of-the-art OOD detectors are highly susceptible to adversarial attacks, which undermines their trustworthiness in automated systems. To address this vulnerability, we apply median smoothing to baseline OOD detection scores, balancing clean and adversarial accuracies. Our key insight is that the noisy samples generated for median smoothing can be repurposed to quantify the local instability of the base score. We observe that OOD samples exhibit higher instability under perturbation. Based on this, we propose ROSS, a novel and robust post-hoc OOD detector that leverages the instability of baseline scores to further distinguish between in-distribution (ID) and OOD samples. ROSS achieves symmetric robustness, performing strongly against both score-minimising and score-maximising attacks, unlike prior work. This symmetric defence leads to state-of-the-art robustness, outperforming prior methods by up to 40 AUROC points. We demonstrate ROSS's effectiveness on extensive experiments across CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and ImageNet. Code is available at: https://github.com/Abdu-Hekal/ROSS.

### [19] [Normalization Equivariance for Arbitrary Backbones, with Application to Image Denoising](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08193)
*Youssef Saied,François Fleuret*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出一种参数无关的“包装器”WNE，可对任意骨干（含Transformer）强制实现归一化等变性（NE），在图像到图像任务中提升对亮度/对比度分布偏移的鲁棒性，并且无额外GPU时延。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实现NE的方法需在网络内部使用受限的NE兼容层（如特定归一化/运算），与常用模块（注意力、LayerNorm）不兼容，且带来运行开销。作者希望既保持NE带来的分布外鲁棒性，又不牺牲模型组件选择和速度。

Method: 理论上刻画NE函数的充要条件：当且仅当函数可被分解为“归一化-处理-反归一化”（normalize-process-denormalize，N-P-D）结构。基于此提出一个输入输出层面的无参包装器（WNE），在不改动骨干结构的情况下，通过对输入做标准化、调用骨干处理、再做反标准化，实现精确NE。

Result: 在盲去噪的单噪声失配诊断上，WNE在CNN与Transformer上均提升鲁棒性，同时几乎无GPU开销；对比的架构级NE方法会导致最高约1.6倍的推理减速。

Conclusion: NE可通过外部包装实现而非内部约束；WNE在不牺牲速度与组件灵活性的前提下带来鲁棒性提升，为将NE普适地应用到现代骨干（含注意力与LayerNorm）提供了实用路径。

Abstract: Normalization Equivariance (NE), equivariance to global contrast and brightness transforms, improves robustness to distribution shift in image-to-image prediction. Existing methods enforce this prior by constraining internal layers to NE-compatible families, limiting compatibility with standard components such as attention and LayerNorm, and adding runtime cost. We characterize the full NE function class: a function is NE if and only if it admits a normalize-process-denormalize factorization. This turns exact NE enforcement, for the ideal wrapper, from an internal architectural constraint into an input-output parameterization problem, allowing a parameter-free wrapper (WNE) to enforce NE around any backbone, including transformers. In a single-noise mismatch diagnostic for blind denoising, the wrapper improves CNN and transformer robustness with no measurable GPU overhead; architectural NE baselines incur up to a 1.6x slowdown.

</details>

### [21] [A Breast Vision Pathology Foundation Model for Real-world Clinical Utility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08207)
*Yingxue Xu,Zhengyu Zhang,Xiuming Zhang,Mengwei Xu,Fengtao Zhou,Yihui Wang,Jiabo Ma,Yi Xin,Danyi Li,Chengyu Lu,Zhijian Cen,Ying Tan,Qingbing Yao,Qi Wang,Zizhao Gao,Yong Zhang,Jingjing Chen,Feifei Liu,Qian Xu,Yi Dai,Hongxuan Tan,Cheng Jin,Huajun Zhou,Zhengrui Guo,Ling Liang,Hongyi Wang,Yingcong Chen,Xi Wang,Zhenhui Li,Ronald Cheong Kin Chan,Ning Mao,Muyan Cai,Zhe Wang,Li Liang,Hao Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: BRAVE 是针对乳腺病理的基础模型，基于10万+全切片图像，在多阶段、多中心、多任务上验证，能在真实流程中安全剔除低风险、救回漏检、并优先级分流；前瞻性与读片者交互研究均显示显著效益，并具预后预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管病理基础模型在回顾性上表现强，但其是否能支撑临床相关应用仍未明，尤其在乳腺癌中，病理评估贯穿诊前、术中、术后，是诊断与治疗决策金标准，迫切需要证明模型在真实工作流中的可用性与安全性。

Method: 构建乳腺自适应基础模型 BRAVE，汇聚来自亚洲、欧洲、北美32个来源的101,638张乳腺全切片图像；在82个队列的34项任务上评估，覆盖穿刺活检、术中冰冻、术后切除。采用循证评估链：回顾性基准测试、临床挑战场景、面向流程的临床影响模拟、阈值锁定的前瞻性观察验证、以及医生-AI 交叉交互研究；并分析模型分数的预后关联。

Result: 在前瞻性三中心验证中：可剔除76.9%的活检阴性（NPV 0.953）和70.1%的冰冻阴性（NPV 0.973）；将78.8%的术后分型案例归为高置信“明确”案例（NPV 1.000）。读者研究中，AI 辅助将平衡准确率从88.5%提升至95.1%（OR 3.14，P<0.001），并提升效率、信心与一致性。BRAVE 分数可独立预测无病生存（调整后HR 4.79，P<0.001）与总生存（调整后HR 8.14，P<0.001）。

Conclusion: BRAVE 在多中心、多任务、前瞻性与交互研究中展现临床可行性：可安全地分流低风险、救回漏检、优先处理关键病例，并提供具有独立预后价值的分数，证明病理基础模型在乳腺癌临床工作流中的实际价值。

Abstract: Pathology foundation models have shown strong retrospective performance, but whether such systems can support clinically relevant use remains unclear. This challenge is particularly important in breast cancer, where pathological assessment serves as the gold standard for diagnosis and guides treatment planning, surgical decision-making and risk stratification across pre-, intra- and post-operative stages. Here we present \textbf{BRAVE}, a breast-adaptive pathology foundation model developed and evaluated using a total resource of 101,638 breast whole-slide images from 32 sources across Asia, Europe and North America. We assessed BRAVE across 34 tasks in 82 cohorts spanning pre-operative biopsy, intra-operative frozen section and post-operative resection, using an evidence chain comprising retrospective benchmarking, clinically challenging scenarios, workflow-oriented clinical impact simulations, prospective observational validation with the thresholds locked in the retrospective cohorts and crossover pathologist-AI interaction studies. Across these settings, BRAVE supported practical roles in the clinical workflow, including safe exclusion of low-risk cases from routine review, AI-assisted second-review rescue of initially missed positives and prioritization of cases for further assessment. In prospective validation across three centres, BRAVE excluded 76.9% of negative biopsy cases (NPV 0.953) and 70.1% of negative frozen-section cases (NPV 0.973), and triaged 78.8% of post-operative subtyping cases as high-confidence clear-cut cases (NPV 1.000). In reader studies, AI assistance improved balanced accuracy from 88.5% to 95.1% (OR 3.14, P<0.001), with better efficiency, confidence and inter-rater agreement. BRAVE-derived scores also independently predicted disease-free survival (adjusted HR 4.79, P<0.001) and overall survival (adjusted HR 8.14, P<0.001).

### [22] [Harmonized Feature Conditioning and Frequency-Prompt Personalization for Multi-Rater Medical Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08210)
*Sanaz Karimijafarbigloo,Armin Khosravi,Alireza Kheyrkhah,Reza Azad,Mauricio Reyes,Dorit Merhof*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一个统一的概率分割框架，利用“采集设备协调+频域标注者提示+GED正则”来分离成像伪影与标注者差异，实现既聚合又个性化的多评者医学分割，并显著提升Dice、GED与不确定性校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多评者医学标注天然存在歧义；现有方法要么做成共识标签要么把差异当噪声，导致模型过度自信、校准差，且设备间伪影与标注风格耦合，无法区分“成像噪声”与“真实主观差异”。

Method: 1) Harmonizer Network：轻量网络隐式建模扫描仪/设备特有伪影，通过自适应特征调制标准化潜表征，使不确定性聚焦于解剖结构而非噪声。2) 高频提示模块（HF prompts）：在频域编码标注者对边界高频与纹理的敏感度，个性化调制经协调后的特征，生成风格化但解剖一致的分割。3) 基于广义能量距离（GED）的正则：将生成分布与经验多标注分布对齐，在分歧处鼓励多样性、在共识处促收敛。4) 在LIDC-IDRI与NPC-170上实验评估。

Conclusion: 通过设备协调与频域个性化相结合，并以GED对齐多标注分布，可同时获得准确、可解释、且校准良好的多评者医学分割，为多专家临床流程提供可靠工具。

Abstract: Multi-rater medical image segmentation captures the inherent ambiguity of clinical interpretation, where diagnostic boundaries vary across experts and imaging devices. Existing approaches often reduce this diversity to consensus labels or treat rater differences as noise, resulting in overconfident and poorly calibrated models. We propose a harmonized probabilistic framework that disentangles acquisition artifacts from genuine annotator variability through adaptive feature conditioning and frequency-domain personalization. A lightweight Harmonizer Network implicitly models scanner-specific artifacts and performs dynamic feature modulation to standardize latent representations, ensuring that uncertainty reflects anatomy rather than noise. To represent rater-specific styles, we introduce a novel High-Frequency Prompt Modules that operate in the spectral domain to encode annotator-dependent boundary precision and textural sensitivity. These prompts adaptively modulate harmonized features to produce personalized yet anatomically consistent segmentations. Furthermore, a Generalized Energy Distance based regularization aligns the generative distribution with empirical annotation variability, promoting diversity where experts disagree and consensus where they converge. Experiments on LIDC-IDRI and NPC-170 show SOTA aggregated and individualized segmentation, with notable GED reductions and improved Dice scores, especially on noisy cases. Beyond accuracy, the model exhibits clinically meaningful uncertainty. Confidence rises in agreement regions and declines in ambiguous areas, supporting its use as a reliable and interpretable tool for multi-expert clinical workflows.

### [23] [Low-Cost Stereo Vision for Robust 3D Positioning of Thin Radiata Pine Branches in Autonomous Drone Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08213)
*Yida Lin,Bing Xue,Mengjie Zhang,Sam Schofield,Richard Green*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 研究探索用一台低成本无人机载双目相机，在无额外深度传感器的情况下，实现对细至10 mm辐射松枝条的可靠检测与三维定位，以支撑自动修枝。提出分割+深度估计两阶段流程，并以质心三角测量结合MAD去噪，将分割掩码与视差图稳健融合为单一枝条距离。实测显示学习型双目方法在1–2 m更连贯，方法具实时性与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手工修枝危险、费工且人力短缺；现有自主修枝系统依赖昂贵LiDAR且仅适用于粗枝，限制推广。需要一种低成本且能处理细枝的感知方案，验证单一低价双目相机是否足以提供精确枝条检测与3D定位。

Method: 两阶段管线：1) 枝条分割：比较Mask R-CNN变体与YOLOv8/YOLOv9，在自建含71对ZED Mini双目图像的数据集上训练/评估，框架保持与新YOLO版本兼容。2) 深度估计：评估SGBM+WLS与多种学习型双目网络（PSMNet、ACVNet、GWCNet、MobileStereoNet、RAFT-Stereo、NeRF-Supervised Deep Stereo），并进行跨数据集微调以揭示城市驾驶到林业场景的域差。核心创新：将分割掩码与视差图通过基于质心的三角测量与Median-Absolute-Deviation离群值剔除，稳健输出枝条到相机的单值距离，缓解林区稀疏纹理、细结构与噪声视差问题。

Result: 定性评估（1–2 m）表明学习型双目深度较传统方法更连贯；所提融合与鲁棒距离估计在细枝（~10 mm）上可行，满足实时与成本约束。并观察到从自动驾驶到林业存在显著域差，微调可改进深度一致性。

Conclusion: 单台低成本双目相机可在林业场景中为自动修枝提供足够精度的枝条检测与3D定位；提出的掩码+视差到单值距离的鲁棒转换是关键。未来可结合更多数据和新一代YOLO/双目网络，扩展距离范围与鲁棒性，并推动替代昂贵LiDAR的实用化。

Abstract: Manual pruning of radiata pine, a species of major economic importance to New Zealand forestry, is hazardous, labour-intensive, and increasingly constrained by workforce shortages. Existing autonomous pruning platforms typically rely on expensive sensors such as LiDAR and are limited to thick branches, which restricts their wider adoption. This paper investigates whether a single low-cost stereo camera mounted on a drone can provide sufficiently accurate branch detection and three-dimensional positioning to support autonomous pruning of branches as thin as 10 mm, thereby removing the need for auxiliary depth sensors. The proposed pipeline comprises two stages: branch segmentation and depth estimation. For segmentation, Mask R-CNN variants and the YOLOv8 and YOLOv9 families are compared on a custom dataset of 71 stereo image pairs captured with a ZED Mini camera; YOLOv8 and YOLOv9 are selected as representative state-of-the-art real-time segmentors at the time of data collection, and the framework is designed to remain compatible with newer YOLO releases. ### [24] [Test-Time Training for Visual Foresight Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08215)

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出T^3VF：在测试时将模型预测的未来图像与随后真实观测视为监督对，进行在线自监督更新；为避免盲目更新带来的灾难性漂移，引入自适应更新过滤机制，仅在置信/一致性等指标满足条件时更新，从而稳定地校正视觉前瞻组件与下游策略。

Result: 实证表明T^3VF以较小的推理开销显著缓解VF-VLA在OOD场景下的性能下降，且无需修改网络结构或引入外部辅助模块。

Conclusion: 利用“预测-观测”天然监督并结合自适应过滤的测试时训练，可有效提升VF-VLA在OOD条件下的鲁棒性与泛化性，具备工程落地优势。

Abstract: Visual Foresight VLA (VF-VLA) has become a prominent architectural choice in the recent VLA due to its impressive performance. Nevertheless, the inherent design of VF-VLA makes it particularly vulnerable to out-of-distribution (OOD) shifts. Because the quality of action directly depends on the accuracy of the predicted future visual information, OOD conditions affect both stages at once. To address this vulnerability, we propose Test-Time Training Visual Foresight VLA ($T^3$VF), a test-time training approach motivated by the observation that the predicted future image and its subsequent observation form a natural supervision pair. To further address the practical challenges that arise from indiscriminate test-time updates, we introduce an adaptive update filtering mechanism. Empirically, $T^3$VF mitigates the OOD vulnerability of VF-VLA at a modest additional inference cost, without requiring any architectural modification or auxiliary modules.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Cardiac magnetic resonance (CMR) segmentation underpins quantitative assessment of ventricular structure and function, yet reliable delineation remains difficult due to low tissue contrast, fuzzy boundaries, and inter scan variability. The search is explicitly resource aware, jointly optimizing dice similarity coefficient (DSC) and 95th percentile Hausdorff distance (HD95) versus model size and floating point operations (FLOPs) under fixed compute budgets. Candidate architectures are instantiated from the supernet, trained with proxy budgets, and evolved through crossover, mutation, and elitist selection. We evaluate on the ACDC dataset and compare against six state of the art methods, using qualitative comparisons, learning curve analyses, and design factor correlation studies. Analyses indicate that searched attention and fusion choices, together with residual scaling, contribute to improved boundary fidelity and stability. CardiacNAS offers a principled, resource aware approach to deployable CMR segmentation with transparent reporting of architectural complexity and compute budgets.

### [28] [TinySSL: Distilled Self-Supervised Pretraining for Sub-Megabyte MCU Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08241)
*Bibin Wilson*

Main category: cs.CV

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出容量感知的蒸馏式SSL（CA-DSSL）：(1) 采用冻结的DINO ViT-S/16作为教师，进行非对称蒸馏，避免小模型被投影头牵制；(2) 多尺度特征蒸馏，显式对齐空间表征，缓解瓶颈；(3) 渐进式增强课程，从弱到强逐步引入增强，降低崩溃风险。以MobileNetV2-0.35为干，预训练于CIFAR-100。

Abstract: Self-supervised learning (SSL) has transformed representation learning for large models, yet remains unexplored for microcontroller (MCU)-class models with fewer than 500K parameters. Standard SSL methods (BYOL-Tiny, DINO-Tiny) collapse entirely at this scale. ### [29] [When Language Overwrites Vision: Over-Alignment and Geometric Debiasing in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08245)
*Harshvardhan Saini,Samyak Jha,Yiming Tang,Dianbo Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文揭示解码式视觉-语言模型（VLM）产生幻觉的几何本质：视觉嵌入过度与文本流形对齐，导致语言偏置压倒细粒度视觉证据；通过从视觉表示中显式投影去除“文本子空间”的主成分，可在零训练和微调两种方案下显著降低多基准上的幻觉且几乎无额外开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM 在医疗、自动驾驶等高风险场景经常“自信胡说”，现有方法要么强行缩小模态差距、要么用代价高的解码启发式抑制幻觉，但都未触及根本成因。作者动机是用可解释、可量化的机制分析，找出导致幻觉的几何原因并提出低成本、通用的补救。

Method: 对解码式 VLM 的注意力对齐过程做机制与几何分析，发现为跨模态对齐而将视觉嵌入过度拉向文本流形，语言统计偏置集中在一个与数据集无关的“通用文本子空间”的前若干主成分。基于此：1）训练-free 推理策略：在推理时将视觉特征在该子空间上的分量投影去除；2）偏置感知微调：在训练/微调中加入同样的投影或正则，显式抑制该子空间的贡献。

Result: 定量刻画了过度对齐和语言偏置集中于通用文本子空间的现象；在 POPE、CHAIR、AMBER 上显著降低幻觉，在长描述任务上提升 CLAIR 分数；训练-free 变体与基线相比基本无额外计算开销。

Conclusion: VLM 幻觉的关键成因是几何层面的“过度文本对齐”。识别并去除集中于顶层主成分的通用文本偏置子空间，可在不增加推理成本或以少量微调的前提下，稳健降低多任务、多基准上的幻觉。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) increasingly power high-stakes applications, from medical imaging to autonomous systems, yet they routinely hallucinate, confidently describing content not present in the input. We investigate the root causes of these failure modes with a mechanistic analysis focusing on the decoder-based VLMs. We trace these failure modes to a geometric over-alignment: to bridge the modality gap required by attention mechanisms, decoder-based VLMs over-align visual embeddings with the text manifold, injecting a statistical linguistic bias that systematically overshadows fine-grained visual evidence. While prior work either aggressively closes this gap or suppresses hallucinations through expensive black-box decoding strategies, none addresses the underlying geometric cause. We provide the first quantitative characterization of this over-alignment, demonstrating that linguistic bias concentrates in the top principal components of a universal, dataset-agnostic text subspace. Building on this insight, we propose two complementary remedies: a training-free inference strategy and a bias-aware fine-tuning paradigm, both of which explicitly project out this subspace from visual representations. Our methods significantly reduce hallucinations across POPE, CHAIR, and AMBER benchmarks, and improve CLAIR scores on long-form captioning tasks, with the training-free variant adding no computational overhead over the base model.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有相似性度量多用于跨样本/跨模型比较，常包含居中、L2归一化与Gram全耦合，这会抹去在单样本内部评估所需的坐标系与幅度信号。作者怀疑冻结基础模型在单图像内拥有稳定的“坐标系”，并想检验这种内部表征是否在不同语义区域保持一致；深伪人脸常在局部逼真却破坏整体结构，天然适合验证该假设。

Method: 提出维度共激活（DCA）：逐维比较两个（或多）语义区域在同一冻结模型特征中的共激活情况。刻意不做居中、不做L2归一化、也不做跨维度的Gram耦合，仅比较相同维度在不同区域上的激活一致性与幅度。使用DINOv3冻结特征，构造如眼-鼻-口的区域指纹进行检测，并做多项消融（加入居中、L2、跨维耦合、或更换模型为FaRL）。

Result: 在深伪检测跨数据集迁移中，基于眼-口-鼻的DCA指纹在CelebDF-v2上AUC=0.9106，在DFD(FF++ c23训练)上AUC=0.9289。消融显示：加入居中AUC降至0.459，L2归一化降至0.862，跨维耦合降至0.478；将DINOv3换成FaRL，CelebDF-v2 AUC降至0.582。

Conclusion: 冻结视觉基础模型内部存在可利用的稳定按维坐标系；DCA能衡量单样本内各语义区域的表征一致性，并在深伪检测上得到强验证。其有效性依赖于保留维度级坐标与幅度信息，而非仅靠区域分割或传统相似性操作。

Abstract: Frozen vision foundation models do not merely extract features; they organize images through a learned coordinate system. We ask whether that coordinate system remains internally coherent within a single input. This leads to Representational Consistency: the study of whether a frozen foundation model represents one sample coherently across its semantic subregions. We introduce Dimensional Coactivation (DCA), a per-dimension instrument for measuring this coherence. DCA compares semantic regions by asking whether the same feature dimensions coactivate across them. Unlike classical similarity measures, it deliberately avoids centering, L2 normalization, and full Gram coupling. These operations are useful when comparing different models or distributions, but they are mismatched to the intra-sample setting, where the coordinate system is fixed and raw magnitude carries signal. Deepfake detection provides a natural validation task. Synthetic faces may reproduce plausible eyes, noses, and mouths while breaking the representational structure that links those regions in real faces. Using frozen DINOv3 features, DCA exposes this break: an eyes-mouth-nose fingerprint achieves 0.9106 AUC on CelebDF-v2 and 0.9289 on DFD under FF++ c23 cross-dataset transfer. The design is also sharply validated by ablation: reintroducing centering collapses CelebDF-v2 AUC to 0.459, L2 normalization reduces it to 0.862, and cross-dimension coupling reduces it to 0.478. Finally, replacing DINOv3 with FaRL collapses CelebDF-v2 AUC to 0.582. DCA therefore depends on a stable per-dimension coordinate system, not on region extraction alone. These results position DCA as an instrument for measuring intra-sample representational coherence in frozen foundation models, with deepfake detection as the first validation task.

</details>


### [32] [Why Do DiT Editors Drift? Plug-and-Play Low Frequency Alignment in VAE Latent Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08250)
*Xiaoce Wang,Sifan Zhou,Kaifei Wang,Leli Xu,Xuerui Qiu,Tao He,Ming Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出VAE-LFA，一种训练免、可插拔的潜空间低频对齐方法，缓解多轮图像编辑中的语义漂移并提升画质与一致性，适用于白盒与黑盒DiT编辑器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮基于扩散Transformer（DiT）的图像编辑会随着轮次累积语义漂移与质量下降。作者从潜空间频域角度分析问题成因，区分VAE与DiT在编辑中的作用，试图找到不需重训即可抑制漂移的方法。

Method: 在VAE潜空间做频域解析：发现DiT主要引入低频漂移且可累积，而VAE带来相对稳定的重建偏差。由此提出VAE-LFA：对跨轮潜向量做低通分解，低频统计与前几轮的指数滑动平均对齐，高频细节保留；无需训练、无需真值先验、无需访问扩散参数。白盒场景将其嵌入管线并减少冗余VAE往返；黑盒场景用现成VAE在轮次间对齐潜向量。

Result: 在多种多轮编辑场景（受控与真实野外图像）上，VAE-LFA显著提升语义一致性与视觉保真度，相比原始流程更好地抑制累积语义漂移。

Conclusion: 语义漂移的主要来源是DiT在潜空间引入的低频偏移；通过在VAE潜空间进行低频统计对齐，可在不重训且适配白盒/黑盒的条件下，有效稳定多轮编辑并保持高频细节。

Abstract: Recent advances in diffusion transformers (DiTs) have enabled promising single-turn image editing capabilities. However, multi-turn editing often leads to progressive semantic drift and quality degradation.In this work, we study this problem from a latent-space frequency perspective by decomposing the editing process into two functional components: VAE and DiT. Through systematic analysis in the VAE latent space, we uncover that the DiT introduces dominant low-frequency drift that accumulates as semantic misalignment across editing rounds, while the VAE contributes comparatively stable reconstruction bias.Based on this insight, we propose VAE-LFA (Low Frequency Alignment), a training-free, plug-and-play method that performs alignment in VAE latent space. VAE-LFA decomposes latent discrepancies across editing rounds via low-pass filtering, and aligns low-frequency statistics to an exponential moving average of previous rounds, effectively suppressing accumulated semantic drift while preserving high-frequency details.Our method requires no retraining, ground-truth priors, or access to diffusion parameters, making it applicable to both white-box and black-box DiT editors. For white-box models, VAE-LFA is seamlessly integrated into the editing pipeline by eliminating redundant VAE round trips; for black-box models, it operates via an off-the-shelf VAE to perform inter-round latent alignment.Extensive experiments demonstrate that VAE-LFA improves semantic consistency and visual fidelity across diverse multi-turn editing scenarios, including both controlled and in-the-wild images.

### [33] [Multimodal Emotion Recognition via Causal-Diffusion Bridge (Affect-Diff)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08252)
*Ankit Sanjyal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Affect-Diff 通过因果加权、VAE 瓶颈与扩散先验联合训练，缓解 CMU-MOSEI 情绪类别极度不平衡问题，在少数类上显著提升平衡准确率与可检测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 Affect-Diff：1) 基于 NOTEARS 学到的因果图，在模态融合前对各模态贡献进行因果加权；2) 使用 beta-VAE 作为潜变量压缩与正则化的瓶颈，控制 KL 强度；3) 引入停止梯度的1D DDPM作为先验，对潜空间进行结构化，防止多数类坍缩。三部分联合训练，另有确定性编码器变体以考察 KL 对少数类敏感性的影响。

Conclusion: 因果加权+VAE瓶颈+扩散先验的桥接式联合训练，有效缓解极端类别不平衡并改善少数类识别；KL 正则强度是调控少数类灵敏度的关键。

Abstract: Multimodal emotion recognition on CMU-MOSEI faces an extreme imbalance as Happy accounts for 65.9% of samples while three Ekman categories collectively represent under 7%, causing standard fusion models to maximize accuracy by ignoring minority emotions entirely. We present Affect-Diff, a Causal-Diffusion Bridge that addresses this through three jointly trained mechanisms: a NOTEARS-learned causal graph that re-weights modality contributions before fusion, a beta-VAE bottleneck for regularized latent compression, and a stop-gradiented 1D DDPM prior that structures the latent space against majority-class collapse. On 3,292 aligned CMU-MOSEI samples, Affect-Diff achieves validation balanced accuracy 0.384, an 18% relative improvement over the strongest baseline (TETFN: 0.324), while all evaluated baselines produce zero F1 on Fear, Disgust, and Surprise. Ablation studies confirm independent, non-redundant contributions from the diffusion prior (-24% without it) and causal graph (-13%). To overcome this fundamental yet underexplored limitation, we propose SAFformer, a novel Spiking Transformer architecture based on an active predictive filtering paradigm. Inspired by the brain's predictive coding mechanism, SAFformer actively suppresses predictable signals and focuses on salient visual features. ### [37] [Is Class Signal Clustered or Routed in Task-Induced Implicit Neural Representation Weight Spaces?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08281)
*Xinyi Guo,Mingyi He,Haobin Ding,Weiming Chen,Xinrui Chen,Jiawen Li,Di Zhang,Minxi Ouyang,Yizhi Wang,Xitong Ling*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文研究在隐式神经表示（INR）框架下，图像被编码为网络权重时，权重空间是否会自发形成按类别聚类；实证发现该几何直觉不成立：即使权重在共享锚坐标下更“类一致”，读出器（reader）性能也可能变差。真正起决定作用的是读出器对权重信号的路由与构造，尤其是SIREN权重token中的“偏置列”作为低维、样本依赖的因果读出通道。基于诊断，作者提出加强路由、显式偏置通道、以及更密集内环拟合等干预，常优于基线但存在非加性交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: INR把每张图像映射为一组网络权重，使分类变成“在权重空间分类”。直观上，若端到端用分类信号训练，图像特定权重应在共享坐标中按类聚类。但这一假设是否真的与分类精度一致、以及读出器如何利用这些权重几何，尚不清楚。

Method: 在SIREN为基的Meta Weight Transformer（MWT）设置中：端到端元学习共享初始化与内环更新以拟合图像特定SIREN；随后分析权重token在共享锚坐标中的几何与可分性；用监督聚类压力与度量学习观察类聚类与读出器精度的关系；通过token-flow诊断追踪读出器各层如何塑造类对齐几何；定位并干预SIREN增强权重token中的“原生偏置列”读出路径；设置对照以排除仅为标量列或边际分布伪影的可能。

Result: 发现：1）原始权重空间的类聚类与最终读出精度并不一致，甚至可能负相关；2）类对齐邻域只有在读出器后期交互后才与精度强相关，输入坐标中并不；3）识别出SIREN偏置列为低维、样本依赖的因果读出通道；4）有针对性的干预（加强路由、显式偏置通道、更密集内环拟合）在文中训练规范下常优于共享锚基线，但相互作用非加性。

Conclusion: INR权重之所以可分类，不是因为它们在原始几何上形成清晰的类簇，而是因为读出器将类别信号通过特定通道进行路由与构造。应将设计重点从“让权重自聚类”转向“优化读出路由”，例如利用偏置通道与更强的读出机制；相应干预能提升性能，但需注意其相互作用的复杂性。

Abstract: Implicit neural representations (INRs) encode images as neural-network weights, making image classification a problem of weight-space classifiability. A natural geometric hypothesis is that classifier feedback should make image-specific weights cluster by class in the shared-anchor coordinate. We test this hypothesis in the SIREN-based Meta Weight Transformer (MWT) regime, where end-to-end training meta-learns a shared initialization and inner-loop update schedule for fitting image-specific SIRENs. We find that this prediction fails. Exposed weight-space geometry and supervised clustering pressure do not reliably track trained-reader accuracy; clustering can even make local neighborhoods more class-consistent while making the trained reader worse. Crucially, the reader constructs rather than inherits class-aligned geometry: token-flow diagnostics show that class-aligned neighborhoods become strongly predictive of trained-reader accuracy only after late reader interactions, not in the input coordinate. We further identify the native SIREN bias column in the augmented weight token as a low-dimensional, sample-dependent causal readout route for the trained reader; targeted controls rule out generic scalar-column and marginal-distribution artifacts. The diagnosis motivates interventions that strengthen reader routing, add an explicit bias route, or use denser inner-loop fitting; under the lane-specific training conventions used here, route-directed variants often outperform the shared-anchor baseline but interact non-additively. Task-induced INR weights are classifiable not because they form raw geometric clusters, but because their class signal is routed through the reader.

</details>


### [38] [Distill, Diffuse, and Semanticize (DDS): Annotation-Free 3D Scene Understanding Based on Multi-Granularity Distillation and Graph-Diffusion-Based Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08293)
*Yijing Wang,Ruonan Li,Qilin Wang,Rongqiang Zhao,Jie Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种无需标注的3D场景语义理解方法，通过多粒度蒸馏与基于图扩散的分割，实现全局一致的语义传播与可解释类别赋名，相比现有方法显著提升oAcc/mAcc/mIoU。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3D点云逐点标注成本高，限制了全监督方法的可扩展性；现有无标注方法能发现语义区域但存在对象级一致性弱、全局聚合低效、结果不具类别语义的问题，亟需一种既可高效全局传播又能输出可解释类别的无标注方案。

Method: 1) 多粒度蒸馏：利用结构化视觉知识指导，将图像侧的丰富语义迁移到3D点云；2) 超点(superpoint)图扩散：在超点图上进行语义扩散，实现高效全局语义传播并提升区域一致性；3) 分割-聚类关联的语义推断：先得到分割的3D区域，再通过聚类与语义对齐为各区域赋予可解释的类别名称。

Result: 在真实世界数据集上，相较先进无标注基线，最高提升oAcc 5.9%、mAcc 8.1%、mIoU 2.4%，验证了框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 该框架在无标注3D场景理解中兼顾对象分割与语义识别，具有可扩展性与实际应用潜力，特别适用于数字孪生、自动驾驶、智慧农业和具身感知等场景。

Abstract: 3D semantic scene understanding has broad applications in digital twins, autonomous driving, smart agriculture, and embodied perception. However, dense point-wise annotation for point clouds is extremely expensive, making fully supervised 3D semantic learning difficult to scale. Recent annotation-free methods can discover semantic regions without manual 3D labels, but they often suffer from weak object-level consistency, inefficient global grouping, and category-agnostic segmented regions. We propose an annotation-free 3D scene semantic understanding method based on multi-granularity distillation and graph-diffusion-based segmentation. The proposed method first leverages structured visual knowledge guidance and superpoint graph diffusion to perform efficient global semantic propagation, alleviating the problem of inconsistent region-level semantics. It then conducts semantic inference through segmentation-cluster association, assigning interpretable category names to segmented 3D regions and improving the overall effectiveness of annotation-free 3D semantic understanding. Extensive experiments on real-world datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework. Compared with the advanced existing annotation-free baselines, our method improves oAcc, mAcc, and mIoU by 5.9%, 8.1%, and 2.4% at most, respectively. These results highlight the promise of the proposed framework for scalable annotation-free 3D scene understanding, especially in real-world scenarios requiring both object segmentation and semantic recognition.

</details>


### [39] [BenchHAR: Benchmarking Self-Supervised Learning for Generalizable Sensor-based Activity Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08296)
*Yize Cai,Rui Feng,Anlan Yu,Baoshen Guo,Zhiqing Hong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: BenchHAR提出统一基准，系统评估自监督学习在可穿戴传感器HAR上的跨分布泛化；发现现有SSL普遍不足，混合式预训练+CNN编码器最泛化，更多无标注同类任务数据比标注数据更有益，非下游类无标注数据无益；定制级设备与肢体到躯干迁移更好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HAR应用广泛但受限于数据异质性与标注稀缺，现有SSL在图像/文本上成功却在HAR泛化方面缺少系统比较与适配策略，需要一个统一框架与大规模数据来量化与分析SSL在未见目标分布上的泛化能力。

Method: 构建BenchHAR基准：汇合集成约258K样本的大规模数据；设计覆盖未见分布的评测协议；在12种编码器-分类器架构上实现并比较8类代表性SSL方法（对比、重构等），并分析数据规模、标签量、活动类覆盖、设备等级与传感器部位迁移等因素对泛化的影响。

Result: 现有SSL方法在跨分布泛化表现不理想；混合范式（重构+对比）总体最优；CNN编码器学到的表示最具泛化性，搭配更强分类器可进一步提升；增加来自下游活动类别的预训练无标注数据显著提升泛化，而增加标注数据收益有限；加入不属于下游活动类别的无标注数据不带来提升；来自定制级设备的数据比研究级设备更易泛化；来自肢体部位的数据较易迁移到躯干位置。

Conclusion: BenchHAR提供评测SSL在可穿戴HAR跨分布泛化的统一基准与实践洞见：优先采用混合式SSL与CNN编码器，重视同类无标注数据规模而非单纯增加标签，谨慎使用非下游类无标注数据，并在设备与传感器部位选择上考虑其对泛化的影响。

Abstract: Human Activity Recognition (HAR) from wearable sensors supports broad healthcare and behavior science applications. However, data heterogeneity and the scarcity of labeled data limit its real-world generalization. Recent advances in self-supervised learning (SSL) in vision and language domains have shown strong capability for learning generalizable representations from unlabeled data. Yet, few studies have systematically compared the generalization performance of SSL methods or explored how to adapt them for generalizable HAR. To address these gaps, we present BenchHAR, a unified framework for evaluating the generalization capability of SSL methods for sensor-based HAR on unseen target distributions. BenchHAR curates a large-scale dataset (~258K samples) and evaluates eight representative SSL methods across 12 encoder-classifier architectures. Our results reveal that existing SSL methods struggle to achieve satisfactory generalization performance. We find that: (1) For HAR models, the hybrid paradigm (combining reconstruction and contrastive pretraining) achieves the best overall performance. The CNN encoder exhibits the strongest ability to learn generalizable representations, while more expressive classifier architectures further improve generalization. (2) For data scale, increasing the amount of pretraining data from downstream activity classes consistently improves generalization, while adding more labeled data yields limited gains. Interestingly, incorporating unlabeled data from non-downstream activity classes does not improve generalization. (3) Sensor data collected from custom-grade devices generalizes better than that from research-grade devices, and data from limb transfers more effectively to trunk positions. BenchHAR provides a unified benchmark and actionable insights for generalizable sensor-based HAR systems. Our code is available at https://github.com/saiketa/HAR-Bench.

### [40] [An Efficient Token Compression Framework for Visual Object Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08329)
*Weijing Wu,Qihua Liang,Bineng Zhong,Haiying Xia,Zhiyi Mo,Shuxiang Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ETCTrack：先压缩再交互的视觉跟踪框架，用自适应令牌压缩与分层交互编码器，在保性能的同时显著减少模板令牌与计算量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer跟踪器为获取更丰富时空线索常引入多历史模板帧，导致视觉token数量暴涨，既带来二次方计算开销，也因冗余特征而降低性能。需要一种能自动消除模板冗余、在不牺牲精度下降本增效的方法。

Method: 提出Compress-then-Interact框架ETCTrack：1) 自适应令牌压缩器（Adaptive Token Compressor），从多历史模板中动态筛除冗余token，生成紧凑且判别性强的模板表示；2) 分层交互编码器（Hierarchical Interaction Encoder），与搜索特征进行深度、自适应的多层级交互，精炼搜索特征以提升定位精度。

Result: 在7个基准上优于SOTA；ETCTrack-B224将模板token减少60%，MACs下降21.4%，精度仅下降0.4%。源码开源于GitHub。

Conclusion: 学习式压缩模板token并分层交互可在保持或提升跟踪精度的同时显著降低计算量，缓解多模板带来的二次方开销与冗余影响，为高效Transformer跟踪提供有效范式。

Abstract: Refining visual representations by eliminating their internal feature-level redundancy is crucial for simultaneously optimizing the performance and computational cost of models in visual tracking. To enhance their performance, many contemporary Transformer-based trackers leverage a larger number of historical template frames to capture richer spatio-temporal cues. However, this strategy leads to a massive number of input visual tokens. This creates two critical issues: it imposes a quadratic computational burden and can also degrade the tracker's overall performance. To bridge this gap, we propose a compress-then-interact tracking framework, ETCTrack, that learns to efficiently compress template tokens from historical template frames into a robust target representation, moving beyond handcrafted rules. Our method first employs the Adaptive Token Compressor to dynamically construct compact yet highly discriminative template tokens by filtering out redundant visual tokens. These refined template tokens are then processed by our Hierarchical Interaction Encoder to achieve a deep, adaptive interaction with the search features. Refined search features ensure subsequent precise target localization. Experiments on seven benchmarks demonstrate that our method outperforms current state-of-the-art trackers. ETCTrack-B224 reduces the number of template tokens by 60%, leading to a 21.4% reduction in MACs with only a 0.4% drop in accuracy. The source code are available at https://github.com/PJD-WJ/ETCTrack.

### [41] [PaceVGGT: Pre-Alternating-Attention Token Pruning for Visual Geometry Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08371)
*Haotang Li,Zhenyu Qi,Shaohan Henry Wang,Kebin Peng,Zi Wang,Qing Guo,Sen He,Huanrui Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PaceVGGT在不改动VGGT主干参数的前提下，于AA前进行令牌剪枝，通过轻量打分器选择并合并重要DINO补丁令牌，在保持重建质量的同时显著降低时延。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VGGT的Alternating-Attention对总token数二次方扩展，使长序列/长视频推理代价高；现有加速大多在AA内部降复杂度，但进入AA的补丁网格仍然臃肿，限制了可扩展性。

Method: 冻结VGGT主干，提出AA前token剪枝框架：1) 从DINO特征训练轻量Token Scorer评估每个补丁token的重要性；先用未剪枝模型在AA内部的注意力作为蒸馏目标进行预训练，再在相机位姿、深度、点图下游损失上微调；2) 为每帧设置固定保留预算，并用“重要性自适应的合并/剪枝分配”在全序列固定合并预算下保留高显著帧的残余内容；3) 通过Feature-guided Restoration模块把稀疏token恢复到预测头所需的致密空间网格。

Result: 在ScanNet-50与7-Scenes上，PaceVGGT在重建质量-时延权衡前沿，推理显著加速；在ScanNet-50上，N=300相较原始VGGT加速5.1×，N=1000相较LiteVGGT加速1.47×，同时维持可比重建质量。

Conclusion: 在冻结的VGGT几何Transformer上，AA前的token剪枝是有效的加速途径；PaceVGGT在保证质量的同时显著降低长序列的推理延迟。

Abstract: Visual Geometry Transformer (VGGT) is a strong feed-forward model for multiple 3D tasks, but its Alternating-Attention (AA) stack scales quadratically in the total token count, making long clips expensive.
  Existing token-reduction accelerators operate inside AA, leaving the patch grid that enters AA uncompressed.
  We introduce PaceVGGT, a pre-AA token pruning framework that prunes DINO patch tokens before the first AA block of a frozen VGGT. PaceVGGT trains a lightweight Token Scorer that estimates per-token importance from DINO features. The scorer is first distilled against an AA-internal attention target from the unpruned backbone, then refined under downstream camera, depth, and point-map losses.
  A per-frame keep budget fixes the backbone-visible sequence length, while an importance-adaptive merge/prune assignment preserves residual content from high-saliency frames under a fixed total merge budget.
  A Feature-guided Restoration module reconstructs the dense spatial grid required by the prediction heads.
  On ScanNet-50 and 7-Scenes, PaceVGGT remains on the reconstruction quality--latency frontier while reducing inference latency.
  On ScanNet-50, it reduces latency by \(5.1\times\) over unmodified VGGT at \(N=300\) and \(1.47\times\) over LiteVGGT at \(N=1000\).
  These results identify pre-AA pruning as a viable acceleration route for frozen VGGT-style geometry transformers.

Method: 提出UIESNN与核心模块MPLB（Multi-scale Pooling LIF Block）：在膜电位动力学中注入分层多尺度池化响应，产生异质、尺度相关的激活，既扩大有效感受野又保留细节；在此之上构建脉冲残差网络，结合频率分解与基于注意力的细化，形成全脉冲管线的增强器。

Abstract: Underwater image enhancement (UIE) is a practically important yet underexplored application of spiking neural networks (SNNs), where the dominant degradations are large-scale and low-frequency, such as wavelength-dependent colour casts and scattering-induced veiling. Existing SNN restoration designs rely on locally bounded spiking perception, which can limit global correction and lead to saturated or inconsistent representations. To address these challenges, we propose a scale-aware SNN framework for UIE named UIESNN. At its core is a Multi-scale Pooling LIF Block (MPLB) that injects hierarchical multi-scale pooling responses into membrane dynamics, thereby enlarging the effective receptive field while preserving fine-grained details and inducing heterogeneous scale-dependent activations. Building on MPLB, we design a spiking residual architecture that integrates frequency decomposition and attention-based refinement in a fully spike-driven pipeline. Extensive experiments on the EUVP and LSUI benchmarks demonstrate that UIESNN achieves state-of-the-art performance among SNN-based methods, delivering improved colour fidelity and spatial coherence with competitive energy cost.

### [44] [Decoupling Endpoint and Semantic Transition Learning for Zero-Shot Composed Image Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08389)
*Mingyu Liu,Sihan Huang,Yijia Fan,Yinlin Yan,Quan Zhang,Jian-Fang Hu,Jianhuang Lai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DeCIR，用解耦的端点对齐与语义迁移学习，结合低秩方向合并（LRDM），在不增加推理复杂度下显著提升零样本组合图像检索性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 投影式ZS-CIR无需在推理时依赖LLM且轻量，但在复杂语义修改上弱于LLM方法。根因在于“语义迁移瓶颈”：端点级匹配易让文本作为目标侧属性提示，而非以源图像为条件的语义迁移。同时，若在同一文本适配器上同时加入端点与迁移监督，会出现端点—迁移冲突，互相牵制。

Method: DeCIR将学习目标解耦：1）从图像-字幕对构造成对的正反编辑元组（forward/reverse），覆盖从源到目标与目标回源的转移；2）为端点对齐与语义迁移分别训练独立的低秩文本适配器分支；3）通过低秩方向合并（LRDM）将两分支融合为一个可部署的适配器，从而保留两种能力且推理开销不变。

Result: 在CIRR、CIRCO、FashionIQ、GeneCIS等数据集上，DeCIR相较现有投影式ZS-CIR方法取得一致性提升，尤其在复杂语义修改上缩小与LLM方法的差距，同时保持轻量与无LLM推理。

Conclusion: 解耦端点与语义迁移学习并通过LRDM合并，可消除端点—迁移冲突，缓解语义迁移瓶颈，使投影式ZS-CIR在不增加推理复杂度的前提下显著受益。

Abstract: Zero-shot composed image retrieval (ZS-CIR) retrieves a target image from a reference image and a text modification without human-annotated CIR triplets. Projection-based ZS-CIR methods are attractive because they do not rely on LLMs at inference and remain lightweight, but they often underperform LLM-based approaches on complex semantic modifications. This gap reflects a semantic transition bottleneck in projection-based ZS-CIR: endpoint-level matching can let the edit text act as a target-side attribute cue rather than grounding it as a source-conditioned semantic transition. We further show that adding semantic transition supervision to the same text adapter creates an endpoint--transition conflict between endpoint alignment and semantic transition alignment. To address this conflict, DeCIR decouples endpoint and transition learning. It constructs paired forward/reverse edit tuples from image-caption pairs, trains separate low-rank text adapter branches for endpoint alignment and semantic transition alignment, and merges them with Low-Rank Directional Merge (LRDM) into one deployable adapter. Extensive experiments on CIRR, CIRCO, FashionIQ, and GeneCIS demonstrate that DeCIR consistently improves projection-based ZS-CIR without increasing inference complexity.

By abstracting execution through an API-driven interface, the system assumes responsibility for secure authentication, resource management, and scalable deployment across diverse high-performance computing environments using Kubernetes architectures. A key innovation of Sci-Orchestra is its autonomous marketplace, which serves as a catalyst for cross-institutional collaboration. This modular infrastructure is specifically designed to facilitate industry partnerships as it provides a secure execution environment and allows external collaborators to test and validate proprietary tools without the need for source-code exchange. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多视频基准多依赖人工标注的真实视频，难以提供精确的时空与物理真值，导致难以诊断模型失败模式。作者希望用可控、可验证的合成环境，系统评估并定位MLLM在多视频推理中的短板。

Method: 构建合成基准 SYNCR，基于 Habitat、Kubric、CLEVRER 仿真引擎生成9,650段视频与8,163组多视频问答，提供程序化验证的grounding。设计8项任务覆盖4个支柱：时间对齐、空间跟踪、比较推理与整体综合。对开源与闭源MLLM进行零样本评测，并分析参数规模与后训练（推理强化）对表现的影响；进行初步的仿真到真实（sim-to-real）相关性分析。

Result: 人类基线为89.5%，最佳模型平均仅52.5%；时间排序相对较好，但在精确的物理与空间推理上较弱，运动学比较任务最佳仅26.0%。参数扩展与推理型后训练能提升时间对齐，但难以改善精细物理跟踪与全局空间综合。部分任务与真实多视频基准的模型层面趋势相关，同时揭示现有评测未覆盖的推理能力。

Conclusion: SYNCR 提供了可控、可诊断的多视频跨流推理评估框架，揭示MLLM在精细物理与空间综合方面的关键短板。未来需要超越单纯参数扩展与常规后训练的方案，以提升物理跟踪与全局空间推理；SYNCR可作为研究与真实场景评测之间的桥梁。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have made rapid progress in single-video understanding, yet their ability to reason across multiple independent video streams remains poorly understood. Existing multi-video benchmarks rely largely on human-annotated real-world footage, limiting the precision of spatial, temporal, and physical ground truth and making it difficult to diagnose model failures. We introduce SYNCR, a controlled synthetic benchmark for cross-video reasoning with programmatically verified grounding. Built using Habitat, Kubric, and CLEVRER simulator engines, SYNCR contains 8,163 multi-video question-answer pairs grounded in 9,650 unique videos. It evaluates MLLMs across eight tasks spanning four diagnostic pillars: Temporal Alignment, Spatial Tracking, Comparative Reasoning, and Holistic Synthesis.
  Our zero-shot evaluation of leading open- and closed-weight MLLMs reveals a substantial gap between current models and humans: the best model achieves only 52.5% average accuracy, compared to an 89.5% human baseline. Models perform relatively well on temporal ordering but struggle with precise physical and spatial reasoning, with the best model reaching only 26.0% accuracy on Kinematic Comparison. We further find that parameter scaling and reasoning-specialized post-training improve temporal alignment capabilities, but do not reliably address fine-grained physical tracking or global spatial synthesis. Finally, an exploratory sim-to-real correlation analysis suggests that several SYNCR tasks track model-level trends on real-world multi-video benchmarks, while also exposing reasoning capabilities underrepresented by existing evaluations. Code available at https://github.com/SaraGhazanfari/SYNCR.

</details>

*Pascal Tilli,Mohsen Mesgar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出在VDR中将全局版式信息以可学习方式注入局部patch表示，不改推理流程，显著提升ViDoRe-v2上的检索效果。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VDR多为late interaction：以局部patch与查询token匹配，效率高但忽视文档的全局版面结构（图表-文本等异构布局），导致仅凭局部相似度易判错。需要让模型感知并利用全局布局以更好评估相关性。

Method: 构建多模态编码器：在保持late interaction推理不变的前提下，用“全局版式嵌入”增强局部patch表示。该全局向量通过文本化的版式描述进行训练监督，使模型学习从视觉布局到语义描述的对齐；最终检索仍以局部-查询匹配执行，但patch已携带全局布局信息。

Abstract: Visual Document Retrieval (VDR) models mostly rely on late interaction architectures, in which documents are represented by a set of local patch embeddings and then matched against query tokens. While efficient, this architecture prioritizes local similarity over global layout structure of documents to estimate relevancy between documents and query. In practice, this leads to errors as relevance originates from layout structure of documents with heterogeneous layouts combining figures, tables, and text. We make document layout learnable without changing inference. We propose a multimodal encoder that augments local patch representations with a global layout embedding, trained via textual descriptions encoding document layout information. Across four ViDoRe-v2 datasets, our model improves over the strongest architecturally comparable ColPali/ColQwen baseline by +2.4 nDCG@5 and +2.3 MAP@5, with statistically significant per-dataset gains over ColQwen.

Method: 提出双诊断框架：FACT用于运动学量化推理的分解诊断，覆盖视觉前提/视觉忠实度、物理定律理解、时间锚定；NICE提出邻域信息引导的校准方法与新指标，用于评估并校准置信度可靠性。对6个最新SOTA VLM进行评测。

This work aims to provide a fundamental understanding of how VLMs perceive the physical world, and utilize physical laws, while assessing the reliability of model confidence. We propose NICE and FACT, a dual-diagnostic paradigm that explicitly decomposes quantitative reasoning for kinematic physics: FACT diagnoses visual fidelity, physical law comprehension, and temporal grounding. NICE studies our novel neighborhood-informed calibration method and novel metrics to evaluate and calibrate confidence reliability. Evaluated across 6 latest state-of-the-art VLMs, we uncover that models fail to identify visual preconditions or utilize necessary physical laws to reach answers. This work highlights and establishes a standardized diagnostic paradigm to guide the development of faithful, physically-grounded VLMs.

Across these settings, CapCLIP consistently outperforms the compared baselines, with particularly strong gains in zero-shot image-text classification and cross-modal retrieval on out-of-distribution datasets. Abstract: Post-disaster situational awareness relies heavily on understanding both the extent and the volume of floodwaters.
